"## Files Examined\n- `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py` \u2014 entry point; contains `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` and `get_select()`\n- `django/db/models/sql/query.py` \u2014 contains `set_values()` which populates `query.selected`\n- `django/db/models/query.py` \u2014 contains `values_list()` and `_values()` which drive the queryset API\n- `tests/select_for_update/tests.py` \u2014 existing tests for `select_for_update(of=...)` with `values_list()`\n- `tests/select_for_update/models.py` \u2014 model definitions (`Person`, `City`, etc.)\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Symptom observed in**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n   `_get_first_selected_col_from_model()` (line ~1440) and `_get_parent_klass_info()` (line ~1424) both do `self.select[select_index][0].target.model`, crashing with `AttributeError` when `self.select[select_index][0]` is an annotation expression (e.g. `Concat`) that has no `.target` attribute.\n\n2. **Called from**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n   `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` (line ~1473) calls `_get_first_selected_col_from_model(klass_info)` for `name == \"self\"`.\n\n3. **Called from**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n   `as_sql()` (line ~884) calls `self.get_select_for_update_of_arguments()`.\n\n4. **Bug triggered by**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n   `get_select()` (lines 259\u2013290) \u2014 `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` is computed with a fixed offset that assumes model columns always appear at positions `[len(extra_select), ..., len(extra_select)+len(cols)-1]` in `selected`. This assumption breaks when `self.query.selected is not None` (i.e. when `values()`/`values_list()` is used with annotation expressions), because annotations can appear before model columns in the `selected` list.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n- **File**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n- **Function**: `get_select()`\n- **Lines**: ~259\u2013290\n- **Explanation**:\n\n  `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` is set unconditionally (lines 262\u2013267) as:\n  ```python\n  list(range(len(self.query.extra_select), len(self.query.extra_select) + len(cols)))\n  ```\n  This encodes the assumption that model columns occupy a contiguous block starting at `len(extra_select)` in the final `selected` list.\n\n  That assumption holds when `self.query.selected is None` (the normal queryset path), because `selected` is built as:\n  ```python\n  [extra_select items, model cols, annotation items]\n  ```\n  so model columns are indeed at positions `len(extra_select)` through `len(extra_select)+len(cols)-1`.\n\n  However, when `self.query.selected is not None` (the `values()`/`values_list()` path), `selected` is built by iterating `self.query.selected.items()` in insertion order. When the user writes:\n  ```python\n  Person.objects.select_for_update(of=(\"self\",)).values_list(\n      Concat(Value(\"Dr. \"), F(\"name\")), \"born\"\n  )\n  ```\n  `set_values()` in `sql/query.py` produces:\n  ```python\n  self.selected = {\"concat1\": \"concat1\", \"born\": 0}\n  ```\n  (annotation alias `\"concat1\"` first, then model-column integer index `0` for `\"born\"`).\n\n  So `selected` becomes:\n  ```python\n  [(\"concat1\", Concat(...)),   # position 0 \u2014 annotation expression\n   (\"born\",    Col(\"born\"))]   # position 1 \u2014 model column\n  ```\n  But `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` is still `[0]` (computed before `selected` is built), pointing at position 0 \u2014 which is the `Concat(...)` annotation, not a model column.\n\n  When `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` later calls `_get_first_selected_col_from_model()`:\n  ```python\n  for select_index in klass_info[\"select_fields\"]:   # [0]\n      if self.select[select_index][0].target.model == concrete_model:\n  ```\n  `self.select[0][0]` is `Concat(...)`, which has no `.target` attribute \u2192 **`AttributeError`**.\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\nThe fix is in `get_select()` in `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`. When `self.query.selected is not None`, track the actual positions of model-column references (integer values in `self.query.selected`) as `selected` is built, then overwrite `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` with those positions.\n\n```diff\n--- a/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n+++ b/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n@@ -279,10 +279,16 @@ class SQLCompiler:\n         else:\n             for alias, expression in self.query.selected.items():\n                 # Reference to an annotation.\n                 if isinstance(expression, str):\n                     expression = self.query.annotations[expression]\n                 # Reference to a column.\n                 elif isinstance(expression, int):\n+                    if klass_info is not None:\n+                        klass_info.setdefault(\"_select_fields_tmp\", []).append(\n+                            len(selected)\n+                        )\n                     expression = cols[expression]\n                 # ColPairs cannot be aliased.\n                 if isinstance(expression, ColPairs):\n                     alias = None\n                 selected.append((alias, expression))\n+            if klass_info is not None and \"_select_fields_tmp\" in klass_info:\n+                klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = klass_info.pop(\"_select_fields_tmp\")\n```\n\nA cleaner version of the same fix (preferred):\n\n```diff\n--- a/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n+++ b/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n@@ -279,9 +279,14 @@ class SQLCompiler:\n         else:\n+            select_fields = []\n             for alias, expression in self.query.selected.items():\n                 # Reference to an annotation.\n                 if isinstance(expression, str):\n                     expression = self.query.annotations[expression]\n                 # Reference to a column.\n                 elif isinstance(expression, int):\n+                    select_fields.append(len(selected))\n                     expression = cols[expression]\n                 # ColPairs cannot be aliased.\n                 if isinstance(expression, ColPairs):\n                     alias = None\n                 selected.append((alias, expression))\n+            if klass_info is not None:\n+                klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = select_fields\n```\n\nThis replaces the stale pre-computed `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` (which assumed model columns come first) with the actual positions of model columns in the `selected` list as built for the `values()`/`values_list()` path.\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Full Execution Trace\n\n**1. User calls `values_list(Concat(...), \"born\")`** (`django/db/models/query.py`, line 1369)\n\n`values_list()` detects that `Concat(Value(\"Dr. \"), F(\"name\"))` has `resolve_expression`, so it generates a synthetic alias `concat1` and calls:\n```python\nclone = self._values(\"concat1\", \"born\", concat1=Concat(...))\n```\n\n**2. `_values()` annotates and calls `set_values()`** (`query.py`, line 1355)\n\n```python\nclone = clone.annotate(concat1=Concat(...))   # adds to query.annotations + annotation_select\nclone.query.set_values((\"concat1\", \"born\"))\n```\n\n**3. `set_values()` builds `query.selected`** (`sql/query.py`, line 2492)\n\nBecause `self.annotations` is non-empty, the `else` branch at line 2509 runs:\n- `\"concat1\"` is in `annotation_select` \u2192 `selected[\"concat1\"] = \"concat1\"` (string ref)\n- `\"born\"` is a plain field \u2192 `selected[\"born\"] = 0` (integer index into `field_names`)\n- `self.default_cols = False`\n- `self.add_fields([\"born\"], True)` \u2192 `self.select = [Col(\"born\")]`\n- `self.selected = {\"concat1\": \"concat1\", \"born\": 0}`\n\n**4. `get_select()` computes `klass_info` with wrong `select_fields`** (`compiler.py`, line 230)\n\n```python\ncols = self.query.select   # [Col(\"born\")]\nklass_info = {\n    \"model\": Person,\n    \"select_fields\": [0],   # \u2190 WRONG: assumes Col(\"born\") is at position 0\n}\n```\n\nThen the `else` branch (line 279) builds `selected` from `self.query.selected.items()`:\n```\nposition 0: (\"concat1\", Concat(...))   \u2190 annotation, NOT a model column\nposition 1: (\"born\",    Col(\"born\"))   \u2190 model column, but klass_info says it's at 0\n```\n\n`self.select` ends up as:\n```\n[0]: (Concat(...), sql, \"concat1\")\n[1]: (Col(\"born\"), sql, \"born\")\n```\n\n**5. `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` crashes** (`compiler.py`, line 1405)\n\nFor `name = \"self\"`, it calls `_get_first_selected_col_from_model(klass_info)`:\n```python\nfor select_index in [0]:                          # from klass_info[\"select_fields\"]\n    self.select[0][0].target.model                # self.select[0][0] is Concat(...)\n    # AttributeError: 'Concat' object has no attribute 'target'\n```\n\n### Why the Fix Works\n\nBy tracking `select_fields` during the `else` branch loop \u2014 appending `len(selected)` (the current position) whenever an integer reference is encountered \u2014 we record the true positions of model columns in `selected`. After the loop, we overwrite `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` with these correct positions.\n\nFor the example above, `select_fields` would be `[1]` (Col(\"born\") is at position 1), so `_get_first_selected_col_from_model` would correctly examine `self.select[1][0]` = `Col(\"born\")`, which has `.target.model == Person`, and return it successfully.\n\nThe fix is minimal (4 lines added in the `else` branch of `get_select()`) and does not affect the `self.query.selected is None` path at all."
